<!DOCTYPE html>
<html id="_top" lang="zh-CN" data-theme="light"><head><script>(function () {
        const storageKey = "theme";
        const root = document.documentElement;
        const supportsMatchMedia = typeof window.matchMedia === "function";
        const mediaQuery = supportsMatchMedia
            ? window.matchMedia("(prefers-color-scheme: dark)")
            : null;

        const readStorage = () => {
            try {
                return window.localStorage.getItem(storageKey);
            } catch (error) {
                return null;
            }
        };

        const writeStorage = (value) => {
            try {
                window.localStorage.setItem(storageKey, value);
            } catch (error) {
                return;
            }
        };

        const applyTheme = (value) => {
            const theme = value === "dark" ? "dark" : "light";
            root.setAttribute("data-theme", theme);
            if (document.body) {
                document.body.setAttribute("data-theme", theme);
            } else {
                document.addEventListener(
                    "DOMContentLoaded",
                    () => {
                        if (document.body) {
                            document.body.setAttribute("data-theme", theme);
                        }
                    },
                    { once: true }
                );
            }
            return theme;
        };

        const updateButton = (value) => {
            const theme = value === "dark" ? "dark" : "light";
            const button = document.querySelector("[data-theme-toggle]");
            if (!button) {
                return;
            }
            const label = button.querySelector("[data-theme-toggle-label]");
            const isDark = theme === "dark";
            button.setAttribute("aria-pressed", isDark ? "true" : "false");
            button.setAttribute("title", isDark ? "切换为浅色主题" : "切换为深色主题");
            if (label) {
                label.textContent = isDark ? "深色" : "浅色";
            }
        };

        const stored = readStorage();
        const initial =
            stored === "light" || stored === "dark"
                ? stored
                : mediaQuery && mediaQuery.matches
                  ? "dark"
                  : "light";

        const appliedTheme = applyTheme(initial);
        updateButton(appliedTheme);

        window.__setTheme = (value) => {
            const theme = applyTheme(value);
            writeStorage(theme);
            updateButton(theme);
        };

        window.__toggleTheme = () => {
            const current =
                root.getAttribute("data-theme") === "dark" ? "dark" : "light";
            const next = current === "dark" ? "light" : "dark";
            const theme = applyTheme(next);
            writeStorage(theme);
            updateButton(theme);
        };

        const syncButtonState = () => {
            updateButton(root.getAttribute("data-theme"));
        };

        const attachToggle = () => {
            const button = document.querySelector("[data-theme-toggle]");
            if (!button || button.__themeToggleBound) {
                return;
            }
            button.__themeToggleBound = true;
            button.addEventListener("click", (event) => {
                event.preventDefault();
                if (typeof window.__toggleTheme === "function") {
                    window.__toggleTheme();
                }
            });
        };

        if (document.readyState === "loading") {
            document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
                syncButtonState();
                attachToggle();
            });
        } else {
            syncButtonState();
            attachToggle();
        }

        const handleMediaChange = (event) => {
            const storedTheme = readStorage();
            if (storedTheme === "light" || storedTheme === "dark") {
                updateButton(storedTheme);
                return;
            }
            const next = event.matches ? "dark" : "light";
            const theme = applyTheme(next);
            updateButton(theme);
        };

        if (mediaQuery) {
            if (typeof mediaQuery.addEventListener === "function") {
                mediaQuery.addEventListener("change", handleMediaChange);
            } else if (typeof mediaQuery.addListener === "function") {
                mediaQuery.addListener(handleMediaChange);
            }
        }
    })();
    if ("serviceWorker" in navigator) {
        window.addEventListener("load", () => {
            navigator.serviceWorker.register("/sw.js").catch(() => {});
        });
    }</script><meta charset="UTF-8"/><meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1"/><meta name="color-scheme" content="light dark"/><meta name="language" content="zh-CN"/><title>2022强网杯青少赛题解 | 花盆</title><meta name="author" content="LittFlower"/><meta property="og:title" content="2022强网杯青少赛题解 | 花盆"/><meta property="og:site_name" content="花盆"/><meta property="og:locale" content="zh-CN"/><link rel="canonical" href="https://blog.littflower.top/writeups/2022-qwbqs-writeup/README.mdx"/><link rel="alternate" type="application/rss+xml" title="花盆" href="/rss.xml"/><link rel="preload" as="style" href="/style.css" type="text/css"/><link rel="preload" as="style" href="/fonts.css" type="text/css"/><link rel="stylesheet" href="/style.css" type="text/css"/><link rel="stylesheet" href="/fonts.css" type="text/css"/></head><body><div class="top-bar fullwidth"><div class="top-bar-inner fullwidth"><div class="top-bar-group"><a href="/" aria-label="root" class="file-link"><img src="/icons/dir.png" alt loading="lazy" decoding="async"/><span>/</span></a><a href=".." aria-label="parent" class="file-link"><img src="/icons/dir.png" alt loading="lazy" decoding="async"/><span>..</span></a></div><div class="top-bar-group"><h3><a href="#_content"><code class="hash inline-code">#</code>内容</a></h3><h3><a href="#_top"><code class="hash inline-code">#</code>回到顶部</a></h3><button type="button" data-theme-toggle="true" aria-label="切换亮暗主题" aria-pressed="false" title="切换主题" class="theme-toggle"><code aria-hidden="true" class="hash inline-code">#</code>  <span data-theme-toggle-label="true" class="theme-toggle-label">浅色</span></button></div></div></div><div class="page-shell"><div class="page-files"></div><div class="page-main"><div id="_content" style="scroll-margin-top:48px;" class="page-article"><h1 id="qwb-2022-wp" class="scroll-target"><a href="#qwb-2022-wp"><code class="hash inline-code">#</code>Qwb-青少赛-2022-WP</a></h1>

<h3 id="misc1" class="scroll-target"><a href="#misc1"><code class="hash inline-code">#</code>Misc1</a></h3>
<p>题目链接：<a href="https://pic.imgdb.cn/item/638eee95b1fccdcd360d0c19.jpg" title="https://pic.imgdb.cn/item/638eee95b1fccdcd360d0c19.jpg" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Link</a></p>
<p>首先拿到一个 png 图片，用 010 editor 查看，根据文件头可以发现它是交换了奇偶数位顺序后的加密图片。</p>
<div class="code-snippet"><pre data-theme="light" class="code-snippet__pre code-snippet__pre--light"><code class="language-yaml language-yaml"><span style="color:#B56959">50 89 47 4E 0A 0D 0A 1A 00 00 0D 00 48 49 52 44</span><br><span style="color:#B56959">00 00 BD 02 00 00 6D 02 06 08 00 00 3B 00 C8 1A</span><br><span style="color:#B56959">00 F7 00 01 49 00 41 44 78 54 EC 9C D9 FD 1C 93</span><br></code></pre><pre data-theme="dark" class="code-snippet__pre code-snippet__pre--dark"><code class="language-yaml language-yaml"><span style="color:#C98A7D">50 89 47 4E 0A 0D 0A 1A 00 00 0D 00 48 49 52 44</span><br><span style="color:#C98A7D">00 00 BD 02 00 00 6D 02 06 08 00 00 3B 00 C8 1A</span><br><span style="color:#C98A7D">00 F7 00 01 49 00 41 44 78 54 EC 9C D9 FD 1C 93</span><br></code></pre></div>
<p>于是第一步解密：</p>

<p>得到新图片为：</p>
<p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" fetchpriority="auto" src="https://pic.imgdb.cn/item/638eee95b1fccdcd360d0c19.jpg" alt="bb"/></p>
<p>关键词“音乐的财富密码”，搜索得万能和弦：4536251</p>
<p>再结合 lsb 隐写，使用 <a href="https://github.com/livz/cloacked-pixel" title="https://github.com/livz/cloacked-pixel" target="_blank" rel="noopener">cloacked-pixel</a> 进行带密码的 lsb 解密即可得到 flag。</p>
<h3 id="misc2" class="scroll-target"><a href="#misc2"><code class="hash inline-code">#</code>Misc2</a></h3>
<p>题目附件：<a href="!%5B1672020979619%5D(image/qwb-%E9%9D%92%E5%B0%91%E8%B5%9B-2022-WP/1672020979619.png)" title="![1672020979619](image/qwb-青少赛-2022-WP/1672020979619.png)">Link</a></p>
<p><del>没太明白，挖坑（</del></p>
<p>明白了，填坑。</p>
<p>要做明白这道题，我们就不得不提一下 2021 年祥云杯上我以为神题的 <a href="https://pan.baidu.com/s/17JzskKNyFEVx79Ozo-dQzQ" title="https://pan.baidu.com/s/17JzskKNyFEVx79Ozo-dQzQ" target="_blank" rel="noopener">shuffle_code</a>，Misc2 与这道题目同理，甚至是它的弱化版（因此建议去做做原版）。</p>
<p>得到的 29 * 29 的打乱的二维码后，通过观察二维码的横向特征或者竖向特征，可以确定这个二维码的打乱方式：如果保留了横向特征，则为打乱行；如果保留了竖向特征，则为打乱列。</p>
<p>在 <a href="https://merricx.github.io/qrazybox/help/getting-started/about-qr-code.html" title="https://merricx.github.io/qrazybox/help/getting-started/about-qr-code.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">这篇文章</a>（可能需要挂梯子）中较为详细地讲解了二维码的特征，同时也可以在这个网站生成一个 29 * 29 的二维码调一调体验一下。</p>
<p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" fetchpriority="auto" src="https://pic.imgdb.cn/item/63a8f2f408b683016327c12f.jpg" alt="定位码"/></p>
<p><a href="https://blog.csdn.net/weixin_45246254/article/details/120491620" title="https://blog.csdn.net/weixin_45246254/article/details/120491620" target="_blank" rel="noopener">这篇文章</a>中展示了如何用 excel 操作二维码。</p>
<p>可以通过确定定位码的方式，确定出题目给的二维码应该是纠错等级为 M，Mask Pattern 为 6 的二维码，根据这个可以确定出前 9 行和后 9 行的二维码。</p>
<p>然后再根据第七列的特征，可以大致填充一下。</p>
<p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" fetchpriority="auto" src="https://pic.imgdb.cn/item/63a9031908b68301633b6b44.jpg" alt="e"/></p>
<p>然后把黑白色的还原后的二维码转为 01 矩阵即可。</p>
<div class="code-snippet"><pre data-theme="light" class="code-snippet__pre code-snippet__pre--light"><code class="language-python language-python"><span style="color:#1E754F">from</span><span =</span><span style="color:#2F798A"> 0.05</span><br><span style="color:#A0ADA0">#等比例缩放</span><br><br><span style="color:#AB5959">def</span><span style="color:#59873A"> get_char</span><span style="color:#AB5959">r</span><span style="color:#B5695977">"</span><span style="color:#AB5E3F">code</span><span style="color:#998418">.</span><span style="color:#AB5E3F">png</span><span style="color:#A0ADA0">#修改图片尺寸</span><br><span style="color:#393A34">im </span><span style="color:#999999">=</span><span style="color:#393A34"> im</span><span style="color:#999999">.</span><span style="color:#393A34">convert</span><span style="color:#2993a3">(</span><span style="color:#B5695977">'</span><span style="color:#B56959">1</span><span style="color:#B5695977">'</span><span style="color:#2993a3">)</span><span style="color:#A0ADA0">#获得二值图像</span><br><br><span style="color:#393A34">txt </span><span style="color:#999999">=</span><span style="color:#B5695977"> </span><span style="color:#CB7676">+</span><span style="color:#4C9A91"> 1</span><span style="color:#666666">,</span><span style="color:#DBD7CAEE"> i </span><span style="color:#CB7676">+</span><span for</span><span style="color:#DBD7CAEE"> body_2 </span><span style="color:#4D9375">in</span><span style="color:#DBD7CAEE"> permutations</span><span style="color:#5eaab5">(</span><span </span><span style="color:#666666">=</span><span style="color:#DBD7CAEE"> pyzbar</span><span style="color:#666666">.</span><span style="color:#DBD7CAEE">decode</span><span style="color:#5eaab5">(</span><span style="color:#DBD7CAEE">im</span><span style="color:#5eaab5">)</span><br><span style="color:#DBD7CAEE">            pbar</span><span barcodes</span><span style="color:#666666">:</span><br><span style="color:#B8A965">                print</span><span style="color:#5eaab5">(</span><span style="color:#C98A7D77">'</span><span style="color:#666666">.</span><span style="color:#DBD7CAEE">show</span><span style="color:#5eaab5">(</span><span style="color:#5eaab5">)</span><br></code></pre></div>
<p>大概跑到 80% 左右就可以爆破出答案。</p>
<h3 id="misc3" class="scroll-target"><a href="#misc3"><code class="hash inline-code">#</code>Misc3</a></h3>
<p>题目附件：<a href="https://pic.imgdb.cn/item/638ef086b1fccdcd36115f1c.jpg" title="https://pic.imgdb.cn/item/638ef086b1fccdcd36115f1c.jpg" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Link</a></p>
<p>根据提示，用 foremost 查看后分离得到 zip，打开得到 secret.png。</p>
<p>依然是带密码 lsb 隐写。<del>（话说考点重复了啊歪）</del></p>
<p>cloacked-pixel 直接解就可以，通过 010 可以查看密码是 <code class="inline-code">7his_1s_p4s5w0rd</code>。</p>
<div class="code-snippet"><pre data-theme="light" class="code-snippet__pre code-snippet__pre--light"><code class="language-shell language-shell"><span style="color:#59873A">python2</span><span style="color:#B56959"> lsb.py</span><span style="color:#B56959"> extract</span><span style="color:#B56959"> ./secret.png</span><span style="color:#B56959"> flag.txt</span><span style="color:#B56959"> 7his_1s_p4s5w0rd</span><br></code></pre><pre data-theme="dark" class="code-snippet__pre code-snippet__pre--dark"><code class="language-shell language-shell"><span style="color:#80A665">python2</span><span style="color:#C98A7D"> lsb.py</span><span style="color:#C98A7D"> extract</span><span style="color:#C98A7D"> ./secret.png</span><span style="color:#C98A7D"> flag.txt</span><span style="color:#C98A7D"> 7his_1s_p4s5w0rd</span><br></code></pre></div>
<p>可以得到 flag。</p>
<h2 id="crypto" class="scroll-target"><a href="#crypto"><code class="hash inline-code">#</code><strong>Crypto</strong></a></h2>

<p>然后使用 <a href="http://quipqiup.com/" title="http://quipqiup.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">quipquip</a> 进行词频分析即可得到 flag。</p>
<p><code class="inline-code">flag{1d817f23-4e20-9405-bf6d-e83d055316d6}</code></p>
<h3 id="crypto2" class="scroll-target"><a href="#crypto2"><code class="hash inline-code">#</code>Crypto2</a></h3>
<p><del>想不明白，不会，先咕</del></p>
<p>flag 格式 uuid，存在 – 字符</p>
<p>多次尝试发现仅需小写字母变动，再把大写字母转为小写...</p>
<p>感觉是 rot 臭题，就硬猜呗？</p>
<h2 id="reverse" class="scroll-target"><a href="#reverse"><code class="hash inline-code">#</code>Reverse</a></h2>
<p>有一说一感觉逆向题目还挺好的（</p>
<h3 id="re1" class="scroll-target"><a href="#re1"><code class="hash inline-code">#</code>re1</a></h3>
<p>go 逆向题，在 ida main_client 中注意到：</p>
<div class="code-snippet"><pre data-theme="light" class="code-snippet__pre code-snippet__pre--light"><code class="language-go language-go">  InputRegisters = github_com_goburrow_modbus__ptr_client_ReadInputRegisters(&v17, 1000, 32);

</code></pre><pre data-theme="dark" class="code-snippet__pre code-snippet__pre--dark"><code class="language-go language-go">  InputRegisters = github_com_goburrow_modbus__ptr_client_ReadInputRegisters(&v17, 1000, 32);

</code></pre></div>
<p>其中 <code class="inline-code">InputRegisters</code> 即为输入的 flag，接下来重点在于 main_enc。</p>
<p>使用 find_crypt 插件 注意到 main_enc 使用的加密算法是 salsa20，一种流加密算法。<a href="https://www.cnblogs.com/init0ne/p/14772868.html" title="https://www.cnblogs.com/init0ne/p/14772868.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">这篇文章</a>详细介绍了这种算法。</p>
<p>参考一般流加密题目的解法，加密过程即是将密钥流与明文逐字节异或得到密文，反之，解密是将密文再与密钥流做一次异或运算得到明文。</p>
<p>动态调试，随便输入 32 位 flag 获得题目程序中的密文，用 ida 把密文数据扣出来，发现其中有不少不可见字符。。。</p>

<p>重新开一次动调，断点到输入之后，目标是把修改的数据改成标准密文。</p>

<p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" fetchpriority="auto" src="https://pic.imgdb.cn/item/63c82d26be43e0d30e472af9.jpg" alt="b"/></p>

<p>用之前获得的标准密文覆盖，然后步过到判断即可。</p>
<p>注意一下大小端序（直接观察也可以），重新修正一下顺序就是 flag。</p>
<h3 id="re2" class="scroll-target"><a href="#re2"><code class="hash inline-code">#</code>re2</a></h3>

<p>flag 长度为 60，注意到 calc 函数的逻辑：</p>

style="color:#CB7676"> +</span><span style="color:#DBD7CAEE"> tmp </span><span style="color:#CB7676">%</span><span style="color:#4C9A91"> 64</span><span style="color:#CB7676"> %</span><span style="color:#4C9A91"> 8</span><span style="color:#d9739f">]</span><span style="color:#666666"> </span><span style="color:#d4976c">)</span><br><span style="color:#666666">    </span><span style="color:#d4976c">{</span><br><span style="color:#DBD7CAEE">      key </span><span style="color:#666666">=</span><span style="color:#4C9A91"> 1</span><span style="color:#666666">;</span><br><span style="color:#4D9375">      return</span><span style="color:#4C9A91"> 0</span><span style="color:#CB7676">LL</span><span style="color:#666666">;</span><br><span style="color:#666666">    </span><span style="color:#d4976c">}</span><br><span style="color:#4D9375">    else</span><br><span style="color:#666666">    </span><span style="color:#d4976c">{</span><br><span style="color:#4D9375">      return</span><span style="color:#DBD7CAEE"> tmp</span><span style="color:#666666">;</span><br><span style="color:#666666">    </span><span style="color:#d4976c">}</span><br><span style="color:#666666">  </span><span style="color:#4d9375">}</span><br><span style="color:#4D9375">  else</span><br><span style="color:#666666">  </span><span style="color:#4d9375">{</span><br><span style="color:#DBD7CAEE">    key </span><span style="color:#666666">=</span><span style="color:#4C9A91"> 1</span><span style="color:#666666">;</span><br><span style="color:#4D9375">    return</span><span style="color:#4C9A91"> 0</span><span style="color:#CB7676">LL</span><span style="color:#666666">;</span><br><span style="color:#666666">  </span><span style="color:#4d9375">}</span><br><span style="color:#5eaab5">}</span><br></code></pre></div>
<p>读到这里就基本可以确定是一个迷宫题目了，并且它的地图是用 tea 生成的。</p>
<div class="code-snippet"><pre data-theme="light" class="code-snippet__pre code-snippet__pre--light"><code class="language-c language-c"><span style="color:#1E754F">  for</span><span style="color:#999999"> </span><span style="color:#2993a3">(</span><span style="color:#393A34"> i </span><span style="color:#999999">=</span><span style="color:#2F798A"> 0</span><span style="color:#999999">;</span><span style="color:#393A34"> i </span><span style="color:#AB5959">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#393A34"> len</span><span style="color:#999999">;</span><span style="color:#AB5959"> ++</span><span style="color:#393A34">i </span><span style="color:#2993a3">)</span><br><span style="color:#393A34">    scr </span><span style="color:#999999">=</span><span style="color:#59873A"> calc</span><span style="color:#2993a3">(</span><span style="color:#393A34">scr</span><span style="color:#999999">,</span><span style="color:#B07D48"> s</span><span style="color:#1e754f">[</span><span style="color:#393A34">i</span><span style="color:#1e754f">]</span><span style="color:#2993a3">)</span><span style="color:#999999">;</span><br></code></pre><pre data-theme="dark" class="code-snippet__pre code-snippet__pre--dark"><code class="language-c language-c"><span style="color:#4D9375">  for</span><span style="color:#666666"> </span><span style="color:#5eaab5">(</span><span style="color:#DBD7CAEE"> i </span><span style="color:#666666">=</span><span style="color:#4C9A91"> 0</span><span style="color:#666666">;</span><span style="color:#DBD7CAEE"> i </span><span style="color:#CB7676">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#DBD7CAEE"> len</span><span style="color:#666666">;</span><span style="color:#CB7676"> ++</span><span style="color:#DBD7CAEE">i </span><span style="color:#5eaab5">)</span><br><span style="color:#DBD7CAEE">    scr </span><span style="color:#666666">=</span><span style="color:#80A665"> calc</span><span style="color:#5eaab5">(</span><span style="color:#DBD7CAEE">scr</span><span style="color:#666666">,</span><span style="color:#BD976A"> s</span><span style="color:#4d9375">[</span><span style="color:#DBD7CAEE">i</span><span style="color:#4d9375">]</span><span style="color:#5eaab5">)</span><span style="color:#666666">;</span><br></code></pre></div>
<p>由于这个 for 循环的性质，所以迷宫的地图是一边跑一边生成，总共有八张地图。</p>
<p>动态调试，输入 <code class="inline-code">uuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuu</code> 以获得所有地图。</p>

<p>然后写个 bfs 走迷宫就好了。</p>

<p>接得 flag: <code class="inline-code">arruuuraaaaarrdbbuuuuuaadrrau</code></p>
<h2 id class="scroll-target"><a href="#"><code class="hash inline-code">#</code>总结</a></h2>
<ol>
<li>可以加/解密码的 lsb 隐写脚本；</li>
<li>词频分析 quipquip；</li>
<li>ida 修改程序内存；</li>
<li>二维码相关知识及爆破脚本的写法。</li>
</ol>
<p>深刻理解了“你电脑上的程序你肯定想怎么改怎么改啊，没有你不知道的。”</p>
